2024-10-13T14:55:28+00:00 - None: from typing import List class Solution:     def count_odd_even_length_subarrays(self, size: int, array: List[int]) -> int:         """         Calculates the number of even-length subarrays with an odd number of odd elements.         Parameters:         - size (int): The number of elements in the array.         - array (List[int]): The list of integers.         Returns:         - int: The total count of valid subarrays.         """         # Initialize a 2x2 matrix to store counts based on index parity and odd count parity         parity_tracker = [[0, 0], [0, 0]]                 # Before any elements are processed, there's one virtual index with even parity and even odd count         parity_tracker[0][0] = 1                 cumulative_odds = 0  # Tracks the total number of odd numbers encountered         valid_subarrays = 0  # Accumulates the count of valid subarrays                 for idx in range(1, size + 1):             current_element = array[idx - 1]                         # Update the cumulative count of odd numbers             if current_element % 2 != 0:                 cumulative_odds += 1                         # Determine the parity of the current index (0 for even, 1 for odd)             index_parity = idx % 2                         # Determine the parity of the cumulative odd count (0 for even, 1 for odd)             odd_parity = cumulative_odds % 2                         # To form an even-length subarray with an odd number of odd elements,             # find previous indices with the same parity but opposite odd parity             opposite_odd_parity = 1 - odd_parity             valid_subarrays += parity_tracker[index_parity][opposite_odd_parity]                         # Update the parity tracker with the current index's parity and odd count parity             parity_tracker[index_parity][odd_parity] += 1                 return valid_subarrays

2024-11-09T15:09:42+00:00 - None: from typing import List from collections import defaultdict class Solution: def maxFrequency(self, nums: List[int], k: int, numOperations: int) -> int: n = len(nums) freq = defaultdict(int) events = [] for num in nums: freq[num] += 1 events.append((num - k, +1)) events.append((num + k + 1, -1)) # Collect all event points and nums[i] values points = set() for event in events: points.add(event[0]) for p in freq: points.add(p) # Sort events events.sort() idx = 0 current_overlap = 0 max_freq = 0 actual_count = 0 for t in sorted(points): # Process events up to current point t while idx < len(events) and events[idx][0] <= t: current_overlap += events[idx][1] idx += 1 actual_count = freq[t] if t in freq else 0 possible_freq = actual_count + min(numOperations, current_overlap - actual_count) max_freq = max(max_freq, possible_freq) return max_freq
